resetPlaceHolder_1(); -> {
  // reset R3
  // reset R2
  if (S1 < R1)
  {
    S1 = R1;
  }
  else
  {
    ;
  }
  R1 = 0;
  C1 = C1 + 1;
  // reset R0
}
use R sep -> R1 = R1 + sep;
use R rep -> R0 = R0 + rep;
use R chunk -> if ((j < 1) || (j == 1))
{
  R2 = R2 + chunk;
}
else
{
  if ((j < 2) || (j == 2))
  {
    R0 = R0 + chunk;
  }
  else
  {
    if ((j < 3) || (j == 3))
    {
      R3 = R3 + chunk;
    }
    else
    {
      R0 = R0 + chunk;
    }
  }
}
